# Off-Season Tech Internships by Pitt CSC & Simplify

We're back! Use this repo to share and keep track of software, tech, CS, PM, quant internships for **Fall 2025, Winter 2026, or Spring 2026**. The list is maintained collaboratively by the [Pitt Computer Science Club](https://pittcsc.org/) and [Simplify](https://simplify.jobs/)!

‚ùó Please note that this repository is exclusively for internships/co-ops in the United States, Canada, or Remote positions üåé

üß† For valuable tips on navigating the internship process, be sure to check out our guide [Zero to Offer](https://www.pittcs.wiki/zero-to-offer) üß†.

üôè **Contribute by submitting an [issue](https://github.com/SimplifyJobs/Summer2026-Internships/issues/new/choose)! See the contribution guidelines [here](./CONTRIBUTING.md)!** üôè
